</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">News release: IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>JPMorganChase To Redeem All $1.6 Billion Of Its </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</FONT></FONT> Rate
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Cumulative</FONT> Preferred Stock, Series X </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Represented By Depositary Shares </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>New York, August</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;20, 2024</B> &#150; JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp; Co. (NYSE: JPM) (&#147;JPMorganChase&#148; or the &#147;Firm&#148;) has
announced that on October&nbsp;1, 2024 it will redeem all of the 160,000 outstanding shares of its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</FONT></FONT> Rate
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Cumulative</FONT> Preferred Stock, Series X (&#147;Series X Preferred Stock&#148;). The shares of Series X Preferred Stock are represented by 1,600,000 depositary shares (CUSIP: 48126HAC4), with each depositary
share representing a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-tenth</FONT> interest in a share of Series X Preferred Stock. The redemption price per share for the Series X Preferred Stock will be $10,000 (equivalent to $1,000 per depositary share). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Payment of the redemption price will be made on the redemption date of October&nbsp;1, 2024, upon presentation and surrender of the depositary receipts
evidencing the depositary shares to be redeemed to Computershare Inc., as Depositary, at 150 Royall Street, Canton, Massachusetts 02021. Depositary shares held in book-entry form shall be surrendered in accordance with applicable procedures of The
Depository Trust Company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">October&nbsp;1, 2024 is also the final dividend payment date for the Series X Preferred Stock and the depositary shares. The
record date for that dividend is September&nbsp;3, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp; Co. (NYSE: JPM) is a leading financial services firm based in the
United States of America (&#147;U.S.&#148;), with operations worldwide. JPMorganChase had $4.1 trillion in assets and $341&nbsp;billion in stockholders&#146; equity as of June&nbsp;30, 2024. The Firm is a leader in investment banking, financial
services for consumers and small businesses, commercial banking, financial transaction processing and asset management. Under the J.P.&nbsp;Morgan and Chase brands, the Firm serves millions of customers in the U.S., and many of the world&#146;s most
prominent corporate, institutional and government clients globally. Information about JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp; Co. is available at&nbsp;<U>www.jpmorganchase.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">#&#8195;#&#8195;# </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
